<pr_description>
[Bug]: Skill short names are exposed but not resolvable by the skill resolver
## Prerequisites
- [x] I will write this issue in English (see the Language Policy)
- [x] I have searched existing issues to avoid duplicates
- [x] I am using the latest version of oh-my-opencode
- [x] I have read the documentation or asked an AI coding agent with this project's GitHub URL loaded and couldn't find the answer

## Bug Description
In an OpenCode environment with oh-my-opencode installed, some superpowers skills are surfaced to the user by their short names (for example `systematic-debugging`), but the `skill` resolver does not actually accept those short names.

Calling the visible short name fails with a `not found` error, and the error message then suggests using the fully qualified name such as `superpowers/systematic-debugging` or the slash-command form `/superpowers:systematic-debugging`.

From a user perspective, this looks like a product bug rather than user error, because the visible skill name is not the same as the executable identifier.

## Steps to Reproduce
1. In the current environment, invoke the skill using the visible short name:
   ```text
   systematic-debugging
   ```
   or call the skill resolver/tool with that same short name.
2. Observe the error:
   ```text
   Skill or command "systematic-debugging" not found. Did you mean: superpowers/systematic-debugging, /superpowers:systematic-debugging?
   ```
3. Retry with the fully qualified name:
   ```text
   superpowers/systematic-debugging
   ```
4. The invocation succeeds.

## Expected Behavior
If a skill is exposed in the available-skills list / UI / context as `systematic-debugging`, that short name should be directly resolvable by the `skill` mechanism.

If short names are intentionally unsupported, then the system should consistently expose only the fully qualified name, so users are not guided toward an invalid invocation.

## Actual Behavior
- The skill is surfaced to the user as a short name like `systematic-debugging`
- The resolver rejects that short name
- The resolver only accepts the fully qualified form such as `superpowers/systematic-debugging`
- The error message teaches the workaround only after the failure happens

## Doctor Output
```shell
$ bunx oh-my-opencode doctor

 oMoMoMoMo Doctor 

 ⚠ 3 issues found:

1. Model override uses unavailable provider
   Provider(s) not found in OpenCode model cache: axonhub, Custom:Nvidia Nim
   Affects: model resolution

2. Comment checker unavailable
   Comment checker binary is not installed.
   Fix: Install @code-yeongyu/comment-checker
   Affects: comment-checker hook

3. Configured models rely on compatibility fallback
   multimodal-looker=google/antigravity-gemini-3-flash (heuristic-backed)
   Affects: multimodal-looker
```

## Error Logs
```shell
Skill or command "systematic-debugging" not found. Did you mean: superpowers/systematic-debugging, /superpowers:systematic-debugging?
```

## Configuration
```json
{
  "note": "No minimal config snippet isolated yet. The issue appears to be in skill name exposure vs resolver namespace handling rather than a user-specific config mistake."
}
```

## Additional Context
My current guess is that the short-name alias is being displayed but not registered in the runtime resolver, or that the resolver is not expanding short names back to the canonical `superpowers/...` identifier.

In other words, the presentation layer and the execution layer seem to disagree about the valid skill identifier.

Current workaround:
- `superpowers/systematic-debugging`
- `/superpowers:systematic-debugging`

## Operating System
macOS

## OpenCode Version
1.3.9


</pr_description>

    27	  plugin: 1,
    28	  config: 1,
    29	  builtin: 1,
    30	}
    31	
    32	function loadedSkillToInfo(skill: LoadedSkill): SkillInfo {
    33	  return {
    34	    name: skill.name,
    35	    description: skill.definition.description || "",
    36	    location: skill.path,
    37	    scope: skill.scope,
    38	    license: skill.license,
    39	    compatibility: skill.compatibility,
    40	    metadata: skill.metadata,
    41	    allowedTools: skill.allowedTools,
    42	  }
    43	}
    44	
    45	function nativeSkillToLoadedSkill(native: NativeSkillEntry): LoadedSkill {
    46	  return {
    47	    name: native.name,
    48	    path: native.location,
    49	    definition: {
    50	      name: native.name,
    51	      description: native.description,
    52	      template: native.content,
    53	    },
    54	    scope: "config",
    55	  }
    56	}
    57	
    58	function mergeNativeSkills(skills: LoadedSkill[], nativeSkills: NativeSkillEntry[]): void {
    59	  const knownNames = new Set(skills.map(skill => skill.name))
    60	  for (const native of nativeSkills) {
    61	    if (knownNames.has(native.name)) continue
    62	    skills.push(nativeSkillToLoadedSkill(native))
    63	    knownNames.add(native.name)
    64	  }
    65	}
    66	
    67	function mergeNativeSkillInfos(skillInfos: SkillInfo[], nativeSkills: NativeSkillEntry[]): void {
    68	  const knownNames = new Set(skillInfos.map(skill => skill.name))
    69	  for (const native of nativeSkills) {
    70	    if (knownNames.has(native.name)) continue
    71	    skillInfos.push({
    72	      name: native.name,
    73	      description: native.description,
    74	      location: native.location,
    75	      scope: "config",
    76	    })
    77	    knownNames.add(native.name)
    78	  }
    79	}
    80	
    81	function isPromiseLike<T>(value: T | Promise<T>): value is Promise<T> {
    82	  return typeof value === "object" && value !== null && "then" in value
    83	}
    84	
    85	function formatCombinedDescription(skills: SkillInfo[], commands: CommandInfo[]): string {
    86	  const lines: string[] = []
    87	
    88	  if (skills.length === 0 && commands.length === 0) {
    89	    return TOOL_DESCRIPTION_NO_SKILLS
    90	  }
    91	
    92	  // Uses module-level scopePriority for consistent priority ordering
    93	
    94	  const allItems: string[] = []
    95	
    96	  // Skills rendered as command items (skills are also slash-invocable)
    97	  if (skills.length > 0) {
    98	    const sortedSkills = [...skills].sort((a, b) => {
    99	      const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
   100	      const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
   101	      return priorityB - priorityA
   102	    })
   103	    sortedSkills.forEach(skill => {
   104	      const parts = [
   105	        "  <command>",
   106	        `    <name>/${skill.name}</name>`,
   107	        `    <description>${skill.description}</description>`,
   108	        `    <scope>${skill.scope}</scope>`,
   109	      ]
   110	      if (skill.compatibility) {
   111	        parts.push(`    <compatibility>${skill.compatibility}</compatibility>`)
   112	      }
   113	      parts.push("  </command>")
   114	      allItems.push(parts.join("\n"))
   115	    })
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  // Sort and add commands second (commands after skills)
   119	  if (commands.length > 0) {
   120	    const sortedCommands = [...commands].sort((a, b) => {
   121	      const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
   122	      const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
   123	      return priorityB - priorityA // Higher priority first
   124	    })
   125	    sortedCommands.forEach(cmd => {
   126	      const hint = cmd.metadata.argumentHint ? ` ${cmd.metadata.argumentHint}` : ""
   127	      const parts = [
   128	        "  <command>",
   129	        `    <name>/${cmd.name}</name>`,
   130	        `    <description>${cmd.metadata.description || "(no description)"}</description>`,
   131	        `    <scope>${cmd.scope}</scope>`,
   132	      ]
   133	      if (hint) {
   134	        parts.push(`    <argument>${hint.trim()}</argument>`)
   135	      }
   136	      parts.push("  </command>")
   137	      allItems.push(parts.join("\n"))
   138	    })
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  if (allItems.length > 0) {
   142	    lines.push(`\n<available_items>\nPriority: project > user > opencode > builtin/plugin | Skills listed before commands\nInvoke via: skill(name="item-name") — omit leading slash for commands.\n${allItems.join("\n")}\n</available_items>`)
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  return TOOL_DESCRIPTION_PREFIX + lines.join("")
   146	}
   147	
   148	async function extractSkillBody(skill: LoadedSkill): Promise<string> {
   149	  if (skill.lazyContent) {
   150	    const fullTemplate = await skill.lazyContent.load()
   151	    const templateMatch = fullTemplate.match(/<skill-instruction>([\s\S]*?)<\/skill-instruction>/)
   152	    return templateMatch ? templateMatch[1].trim() : fullTemplate
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  if (skill.scope === "config" && skill.definition.template) {
   156	    const templateMatch = skill.definition.template.match(/<skill-instruction>([\s\S]*?)<\/skill-instruction>/)
   157	    return templateMatch ? templateMatch[1].trim() : skill.definition.template
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  if (skill.path) {
   161	    return extractSkillTemplate(skill)
   162	  }
   163	
   164	  const templateMatch = skill.definition.template?.match(/<skill-instruction>([\s\S]*?)<\/skill-instruction>/)
   165	  return templateMatch ? templateMatch[1].trim() : skill.definition.template || ""
   166	}
   167	
   168	async function formatMcpCapabilities(
   169	  skill: LoadedSkill,
   170	  manager: SkillMcpManager,
   171	  sessionID: string
   172	): Promise<string | null> {
   173	  if (!skill.mcpConfig || Object.keys(skill.mcpConfig).length === 0) {
   174	    return null
   175	  }
   176	
   177	  const sections: string[] = ["", "## Available MCP Servers", ""]
   178	
   179	  for (const [serverName, config] of Object.entries(skill.mcpConfig)) {
   180	    const info: SkillMcpClientInfo = {
   181	      serverName,
   182	      skillName: skill.name,
   183	      sessionID,
   184	    }
   185	    const context: SkillMcpServerContext = {
   186	      config,
   187	      skillName: skill.name,
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    sections.push(`### ${serverName}`)
   191	    sections.push("")
   192	
   193	    try {
   194	      const [tools, resources, prompts] = await Promise.all([
   195	        manager.listTools(info, context).catch(() => []),
   196	        manager.listResources(info, context).catch(() => []),
   197	        manager.listPrompts(info, context).catch(() => []),
   198	      ])
   199	
   200	      if (tools.length > 0) {
   201	        sections.push("**Tools:**")
   202	        sections.push("")
   203	        for (const t of tools as Tool[]) {
   204	          sections.push(`#### \`${t.name}\``)
   205	          if (t.description) {
   206	            sections.push(t.description)
   207	          }
   208	          sections.push("")
   209	          sections.push("**inputSchema:**")
   210	          sections.push("```json")
   211	          sections.push(JSON.stringify(sanitizeJsonSchema(t.inputSchema), null, 2))
   212	          sections.push("```")
   213	          sections.push("")
   214	        }
   215	      }
   216	      if (resources.length > 0) {
   217	        sections.push(`**Resources**: ${resources.map((r: Resource) => r.uri).join(", ")}`)
   218	      }
   219	      if (prompts.length > 0) {
   220	        sections.push(`**Prompts**: ${prompts.map((p: Prompt) => p.name).join(", ")}`)
   221	      }
   222	
   223	      if (tools.length === 0 && resources.length === 0 && prompts.length === 0) {
   224	        sections.push("*No capabilities discovered*")
   225	      }
   226	    } catch (error) {
   227	      const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
   228	      sections.push(`*Failed to connect: ${errorMessage.split("\n")[0]}*`)
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    sections.push("")
   232	    sections.push(`Use \`skill_mcp\` tool with \`mcp_name="${serverName}"\` to invoke.`)
   233	    sections.push("")
   234	  }
   235	
   236	  return sections.join("\n")
   237	}
   238	
   239	export function createSkillTool(options: SkillLoadOptions = {}): ToolDefinition {
   240	  let cachedDescription: string | null = null
   241	
   242	  const getSkills = async (): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> => {
   243	    clearSkillCache()
   244	    const discovered = await getAllSkills({disabledSkills: options?.disabledSkills, browserProvider: options?.browserProvider})
   245	    const allSkills = !options.skills
   246	      ? discovered
   247	      : [...discovered, ...options.skills.filter(s => !new Set(discovered.map(d => d.name)).has(s.name))]
   248	
   249	    if (options.nativeSkills) {
   250	      try {
   251	        const nativeAll = await options.nativeSkills.all()
   252	        mergeNativeSkills(allSkills, nativeAll)
   253	      } catch {
   254	        // Native skill discovery may not be available
   255	      }
   256	    }
   257	
   258	    return allSkills
   259	  }
   260	
   261	  const getCommands = (): CommandInfo[] => {
   262	    return discoverCommandsSync(undefined, {
   263	      pluginsEnabled: options.pluginsEnabled,
   264	      enabledPluginsOverride: options.enabledPluginsOverride,
   265	    })
   266	  }
   267	
   268	  const buildDescription = async (force = false): Promise<string> => {
   269	    if (!force && cachedDescription) return cachedDescription
   270	    const skills = await getSkills()
   271	    const commands = getCommands()
   272	    const skillInfos = skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo)
   273	    cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skillInfos, commands)
   274	    return cachedDescription
   275	  }
   276	
   277	  if (options.skills !== undefined) {
   278	    const skillInfos = options.skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo)
   279	    const commandsForDescription = options.commands ?? []
   280	    let needsAsyncRefresh = false
   281	
   282	    if (options.nativeSkills) {
   283	      try {
   284	        const nativeAll = options.nativeSkills.all()
   285	        if (isPromiseLike(nativeAll)) {
   286	          needsAsyncRefresh = true
   287	        } else {
   288	          mergeNativeSkillInfos(skillInfos, nativeAll)
   289	        }
   290	      } catch {
   291	        // Native skill discovery may not be available
   292	      }
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skillInfos, commandsForDescription)
   296	    if (needsAsyncRefresh) {
   297	      void buildDescription(true)
   298	    }
   299	  } else if (options.commands !== undefined) {
   300	    cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription([], options.commands)
   301	  } else {
   302	    void buildDescription()
   303	  }
   304	
   305	  return tool({
   306	    get description() {
   307	      if (cachedDescription === null) {
   308	        void buildDescription()
   309	      }
   310	      return cachedDescription ?? TOOL_DESCRIPTION_PREFIX
   311	    },
   312	    args: {
   313	      name: tool.schema.string().describe("The skill or command name (e.g., 'code-review' or 'publish'). Use without leading slash for commands."),
   314	      user_message: tool.schema
   315	        .string()
   316	        .optional()
   317	        .describe("Optional arguments or context for command invocation. Example: name='publish', user_message='patch'"),
   318	    },
   319	    async execute(args: SkillArgs, ctx?: { agent?: string }) {
   320	      const skills = await getSkills()
   321	      const commands = getCommands()
   322	      cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo), commands)
   323	
   324	      const requestedName = args.name.replace(/^\//, "")
   325	
   326	      // Check skills first (exact match, case-insensitive)
   327	      const matchedSkill = skills.find(s => s.name.toLowerCase() === requestedName.toLowerCase())
   328	
   329	      if (matchedSkill) {
   330	        if (matchedSkill.definition.agent && (!ctx?.agent || matchedSkill.definition.agent !== ctx.agent)) {
   331	          throw new Error(`Skill "${matchedSkill.name}" is restricted to agent "${matchedSkill.definition.agent}"`)
   332	        }
   333	
   334	        let body = await extractSkillBody(matchedSkill)
   335	
   336	        if (matchedSkill.name === "git-master") {
   337	          body = injectGitMasterConfig(body, options.gitMasterConfig)
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        const dir = matchedSkill.path ? dirname(matchedSkill.path) : matchedSkill.resolvedPath || process.cwd()
   341	
   342	        const output = [
   343	          `## Skill: ${matchedSkill.name}`,
   344	          "",
   345	          `**Base directory**: ${dir}`,
   346	          "",
   347	          body,
   348	        ]
   349	
   350	        if (options.mcpManager && options.getSessionID && matchedSkill.mcpConfig) {
   351	          const mcpInfo = await formatMcpCapabilities(
   352	            matchedSkill,
   353	            options.mcpManager,
   354	            options.getSessionID()
   355	          )
   356	          if (mcpInfo) {
   357	            output.push(mcpInfo)
   358	          }
   359	        }
   360	
   361	        return output.join("\n")
   362	      }
   363	
   364	      // Check commands (exact match, case-insensitive) - sort by priority first
   365	      const sortedCommands = [...commands].sort((a, b) => {
   366	        const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
   367	        const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
   368	        return priorityB - priorityA // Higher priority first
   369	      })
   370	      const matchedCommand = sortedCommands.find(c => c.name.toLowerCase() === requestedName.toLowerCase())
   371	
   372	      if (matchedCommand) {
   373	        return await formatLoadedCommand(matchedCommand, args.user_message)
   374	      }
   375	
   376	      // No match found — provide helpful error with partial matches
   377	      const allNames = [
   378	        ...skills.map(s => s.name),
   379	        ...commands.map(c => `/${c.name}`),
   380	      ]
   381	
   382	      const partialMatches = allNames.filter(n =>
   383	        n.toLowerCase().includes(requestedName.toLowerCase())
   384	      )
   385	
   386	      if (partialMatches.length > 0) {
   387	        throw new Error(
   388	          `Skill or command "${args.name}" not found. Did you mean: ${partialMatches.join(", ")}?`
   389	        )
   390	      }
   391	
   392	      const available = allNames.join(", ")
   393	      throw new Error(
   394	        `Skill or command "${args.name}" not found. Available: ${available || "none"}`
   395	      )
   396	    },
   397	  })
   398	}
   399	
   400	export const skill: ToolDefinition = createSkillTool()
   401

     9	import type { CommandDefinition } from "../claude-code-command-loader/types"
    10	import type { SkillScope, SkillMetadata, LoadedSkill } from "./types"
    11	import type { SkillMcpConfig } from "../skill-mcp-manager/types"
    12	
    13	export async function mapWithConcurrency<T, R>(
    14	  items: T[],
    15	  mapper: (item: T) => Promise<R>,
    16	  concurrency: number
    17	): Promise<R[]> {
    18	  const results: R[] = new Array(items.length)
    19	  let index = 0
    20	  
    21	  const worker = async () => {
    22	    while (index < items.length) {
    23	      const currentIndex = index++
    24	      results[currentIndex] = await mapper(items[currentIndex])
    25	    }
    26	  }
    27	  
    28	  const workers = Array.from({ length: Math.min(concurrency, items.length) }, () => worker())
    29	  await Promise.all(workers)
    30	  
    31	  return results
    32	}
    33	
    34	function parseSkillMcpConfigFromFrontmatter(content: string): SkillMcpConfig | undefined {
    35	  const frontmatterMatch = content.match(/^---\r?\n([\s\S]*?)\r?\n---/)
    36	  if (!frontmatterMatch) return undefined
    37	
    38	  try {
    39	    const parsed = yaml.load(frontmatterMatch[1]) as Record<string, unknown>
    40	    if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && "mcp" in parsed && parsed.mcp) {
    41	      return parsed.mcp as SkillMcpConfig
    42	    }
    43	  } catch {
    44	    return undefined
    45	  }
    46	  return undefined
    47	}
    48	
    49	export async function loadMcpJsonFromDirAsync(skillDir: string): Promise<SkillMcpConfig | undefined> {
    50	  const mcpJsonPath = join(skillDir, "mcp.json")
    51	
    52	  try {
    53	    const content = await readFile(mcpJsonPath, "utf-8")
    54	    const parsed = JSON.parse(content) as Record<string, unknown>
    55	    
    56	    if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && "mcpServers" in parsed && parsed.mcpServers) {
    57	      return parsed.mcpServers as SkillMcpConfig
    58	    }
    59	    
    60	    if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && !("mcpServers" in parsed)) {
    61	      const hasCommandField = Object.values(parsed).some(
    62	        (v) => v && typeof v === "object" && "command" in (v as Record<string, unknown>)
    63	      )
    64	      if (hasCommandField) {
    65	        return parsed as SkillMcpConfig
    66	      }
    67	    }
    68	  } catch {
    69	    return undefined
    70	  }
    71	  return undefined
    72	}

    74	export async function loadSkillFromPathAsync(
    75	  skillPath: string,
    76	  resolvedPath: string,
    77	  defaultName: string,
    78	  scope: SkillScope,
    79	  namePrefix = ""
    80	): Promise<LoadedSkill | null> {
    81	  try {
    82	    const content = await readFile(skillPath, "utf-8")
    83	    const { data, body, parseError } = parseFrontmatter<SkillMetadata>(content)
    84	    if (parseError) return null
    85	    
    86	    const frontmatterMcp = parseSkillMcpConfigFromFrontmatter(content)
    87	    const mcpJsonMcp = await loadMcpJsonFromDirAsync(resolvedPath)
    88	    const mcpConfig = mcpJsonMcp || frontmatterMcp
    89	
    90	    const baseName = data.name || defaultName
    91	    const skillName = namePrefix ? `${namePrefix}/${baseName}` : baseName
    92	    const originalDescription = data.description || ""
    93	    const isOpencodeSource = scope === "opencode" || scope === "opencode-project"
    94	    const formattedDescription = `(${scope} - Skill) ${originalDescription}`
    95	
    96	    const resolvedBody = resolveSkillPathReferences(body.trim(), resolvedPath)

    98	Base directory for this skill: ${resolvedPath}/
    99	File references (@path) in this skill are relative to this directory.
   100	
   101	${resolvedBody}
   102	</skill-instruction>
   103	
   104	<user-request>
   105	$ARGUMENTS
   106	</user-request>`
   107	
   108	    const definition: CommandDefinition = {
   109	      name: skillName,
   110	      description: formattedDescription,
   111	      template: wrappedTemplate,
   112	      model: sanitizeModelField(data.model, isOpencodeSource ? "opencode" : "claude-code"),
   113	      agent: data.agent,

   116	    }
   117	
   118	    return {
   119	      name: skillName,
   120	      path: skillPath,
   121	      resolvedPath,
   122	      definition,
   123	      scope,
   124	      license: data.license,
   125	      compatibility: data.compatibility,
   126	      metadata: data.metadata,
   127	      allowedTools: parseAllowedTools(data["allowed-tools"]),
   128	      mcpConfig,
   129	    }
   130	  } catch {
   131	    return null
   132	  }
   133	}
   134	
   135	function parseAllowedTools(allowedTools: string | string[] | undefined): string[] | undefined {
   136	  if (!allowedTools) return undefined
   137	  
   138	  // Handle YAML array format: already parsed as string[]
   139	  if (Array.isArray(allowedTools)) {
   140	    return allowedTools.map(t => t.trim()).filter(Boolean)
   141	  }
   142	  
   143	  // Handle space-separated string format: "Read Write Edit Bash"
   144	  return allowedTools.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean)
   145	}
   146	
   147	export async function discoverSkillsInDirAsync(
   148	  skillsDir: string,
   149	  scope: SkillScope = "opencode-project",
   150	  namePrefix = "",
   151	  depth = 0,
   152	  maxDepth = 2
   153	): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> {
   154	  try {
   155	    const entries = await readdir(skillsDir, { withFileTypes: true })
   156	    
   157	    const processEntry = async (entry: Dirent): Promise<LoadedSkill | LoadedSkill[] | null> => {
   158	      if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) return null
   159	
   160	      const entryPath = join(skillsDir, entry.name)
   161	
   162	      if (entry.isDirectory() || entry.isSymbolicLink()) {
   163	        const resolvedPath = resolveSymlink(entryPath)
   164	        const dirName = entry.name
   165	
   166	        const skillMdPath = join(resolvedPath, "SKILL.md")
   167	        try {
   168	          await readFile(skillMdPath, "utf-8")
   169	          return await loadSkillFromPathAsync(skillMdPath, resolvedPath, dirName, scope, namePrefix)
   170	        } catch {
   171	          const namedSkillMdPath = join(resolvedPath, `${dirName}.md`)
   172	          try {
   173	            await readFile(namedSkillMdPath, "utf-8")
   174	            return await loadSkillFromPathAsync(namedSkillMdPath, resolvedPath, dirName, scope, namePrefix)
   175	          } catch {
   176	            if (depth >= maxDepth) {
   177	              return null
   178	            }
   179	
   180	            const nestedPrefix = namePrefix ? `${namePrefix}/${dirName}` : dirName
   181	            const nestedSkills = await discoverSkillsInDirAsync(
   182	              resolvedPath,
   183	              scope,
   184	              nestedPrefix,
   185	              depth + 1,
   186	              maxDepth
   187	            )
   188	
   189	            return nestedSkills.length > 0 ? nestedSkills : null
   190	          }
   191	        }
   192	      }
   193	
   194	      if (isMarkdownFile(entry)) {
   195	        const skillName = basename(entry.name, ".md")
   196	        return await loadSkillFromPathAsync(entryPath, skillsDir, skillName, scope, namePrefix)
   197	      }
   198	
   199	      return null
   200	    }
   201	
   202	    const skillPromises = await mapWithConcurrency(entries, processEntry, 16)
   203	    return skillPromises.flatMap((skill): LoadedSkill[] => {
   204	      if (skill === null) return []
   205	      return Array.isArray(skill) ? skill : [skill]
   206	    })
   207	  } catch (error: unknown) {
   208	    if (error && typeof error === "object" && "code" in error && error.code === "ENOENT") {
   209	      return []
   210	    }
   211	    return []
   212	  }
   213	}
   214

import type { LazyContentLoader } from "../../features/opencode-skill-loader"

export type CommandScope = "builtin" | "config" | "user" | "project" | "opencode" | "opencode-project" | "plugin"

export interface CommandMetadata {
  name: string
  description: string
  argumentHint?: string
  model?: string
  agent?: string
  subtask?: boolean
}

export interface CommandInfo {
  name: string
  path?: string
  metadata: CommandMetadata
  content?: string
  scope: CommandScope
  lazyContentLoader?: LazyContentLoader
}
import { existsSync, readdirSync, readFileSync } from "fs"
import { basename, join } from "path"
import {
  parseFrontmatter,
  sanitizeModelField,
  findProjectOpencodeCommandDirs,
  getOpenCodeCommandDirs,
  discoverPluginCommandDefinitions,
} from "../../shared"
import type { CommandFrontmatter } from "../../features/claude-code-command-loader/types"
import { isMarkdownFile } from "../../shared/file-utils"
import { getClaudeConfigDir } from "../../shared"
import { loadBuiltinCommands } from "../../features/builtin-commands"
import type { CommandInfo, CommandMetadata, CommandScope } from "./types"

export interface CommandDiscoveryOptions {
  pluginsEnabled?: boolean
  enabledPluginsOverride?: Record<string, boolean>
}

const NESTED_COMMAND_SEPARATOR = "/"

function discoverCommandsFromDir(
  commandsDir: string,
  scope: CommandScope,
  prefix = "",
): CommandInfo[] {
  if (!existsSync(commandsDir)) return []

  const entries = readdirSync(commandsDir, { withFileTypes: true })
  const commands: CommandInfo[] = []

  for (const entry of entries) {
    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue
      const nestedPrefix = prefix
        ? `${prefix}${NESTED_COMMAND_SEPARATOR}${entry.name}`
        : entry.name
      commands.push(
        ...discoverCommandsFromDir(join(commandsDir, entry.name), scope, nestedPrefix),
      )
      continue
    }

    if (!isMarkdownFile(entry)) continue

    const commandPath = join(commandsDir, entry.name)
    const baseCommandName = basename(entry.name, ".md")
    const commandName = prefix
      ? `${prefix}${NESTED_COMMAND_SEPARATOR}${baseCommandName}`
      : baseCommandName

    try {
      const content = readFileSync(commandPath, "utf-8")
      const { data, body } = parseFrontmatter<CommandFrontmatter>(content)

      const isOpencodeSource = scope === "opencode" || scope === "opencode-project"
      const metadata: CommandMetadata = {
        name: commandName,
        description: data.description || "",
        argumentHint: data["argument-hint"],
        model: sanitizeModelField(data.model, isOpencodeSource ? "opencode" : "claude-code"),
        agent: data.agent,
        subtask: Boolean(data.subtask),
      }

      commands.push({
        name: commandName,
        path: commandPath,
        metadata,
        content: body,
        scope,
      })
    } catch {
      continue
    }
  }

  return commands
}

function discoverPluginCommands(options?: CommandDiscoveryOptions): CommandInfo[] {
  const pluginDefinitions = discoverPluginCommandDefinitions(options)

  return Object.entries(pluginDefinitions).map(([name, definition]) => ({
    name,
    metadata: {
      name,
      description: definition.description || "",
      model: definition.model,
      agent: definition.agent,
      subtask: definition.subtask,
    },
    content: definition.template,
    scope: "plugin",
  }))
}

function deduplicateCommandInfosByName(commands: CommandInfo[]): CommandInfo[] {
  const seen = new Set<string>()
  const deduplicatedCommands: CommandInfo[] = []

  for (const command of commands) {
    if (seen.has(command.name)) {
      continue
    }

    seen.add(command.name)
    deduplicatedCommands.push(command)
  }

  return deduplicatedCommands
}

export function discoverCommandsSync(
  directory?: string,
  options?: CommandDiscoveryOptions,
): CommandInfo[] {
  const userCommandsDir = join(getClaudeConfigDir(), "commands")
  const projectCommandsDir = join(directory ?? process.cwd(), ".claude", "commands")
  const opencodeGlobalDirs = getOpenCodeCommandDirs({ binary: "opencode" })
  const opencodeProjectDirs = findProjectOpencodeCommandDirs(directory ?? process.cwd())

  const userCommands = discoverCommandsFromDir(userCommandsDir, "user")
  const opencodeGlobalCommands = opencodeGlobalDirs.flatMap((commandsDir) =>
    discoverCommandsFromDir(commandsDir, "opencode")
  )
  const projectCommands = discoverCommandsFromDir(projectCommandsDir, "project")
  const opencodeProjectCommands = opencodeProjectDirs.flatMap((commandsDir) =>
    discoverCommandsFromDir(commandsDir, "opencode-project"),
  )
  const pluginCommands = discoverPluginCommands(options)

  const builtinCommandsMap = loadBuiltinCommands()
  const builtinCommands: CommandInfo[] = Object.values(builtinCommandsMap).map((command) => ({
    name: command.name,
    metadata: {
      name: command.name,
      description: command.description || "",
      argumentHint: command.argumentHint,
      model: command.model,
      agent: command.agent,
      subtask: command.subtask,
    },
    content: command.template,
    scope: "builtin",
  }))

  return deduplicateCommandInfosByName([
    ...projectCommands,
    ...userCommands,
    ...opencodeProjectCommands,
    ...opencodeGlobalCommands,
    ...builtinCommands,
    ...pluginCommands,
  ])
}

    22	export type SkillContext = {
    23	  mergedSkills: LoadedSkill[]
    24	  availableSkills: AvailableSkill[]

    29	const PROVIDER_GATED_SKILL_NAMES = new Set(["agent-browser", "playwright"])
    30	
    31	function mapScopeToLocation(scope: SkillScope): AvailableSkill["location"] {
    32	  if (scope === "user" || scope === "opencode") return "user"
    33	  if (scope === "project" || scope === "opencode-project") return "project"
    34	  return "plugin"
    35	}
    36	
    37	function filterProviderGatedSkills(
    38	  skills: LoadedSkill[],
    39	  browserProvider: BrowserAutomationProvider,
    40	): LoadedSkill[] {
    41	  return skills.filter((skill) => {
    42	    if (!PROVIDER_GATED_SKILL_NAMES.has(skill.name)) {
    43	      return true
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    return skill.name === browserProvider
    47	  })
    48	}
    49	
    50	export async function createSkillContext(args: {
    51	  directory: string
    52	  pluginConfig: OhMyOpenCodeConfig
    53	}): Promise<SkillContext> {
    54	  const { directory, pluginConfig } = args
    55	
    56	  const browserProvider: BrowserAutomationProvider =
    57	    pluginConfig.browser_automation_engine?.provider ?? "playwright"
    58	
    59	  const disabledSkills = new Set<string>(pluginConfig.disabled_skills ?? [])
    60	  const systemMcpNames = getSystemMcpServerNames()
    61	
    62	  const builtinSkills = createBuiltinSkills({
    63	    browserProvider,
    64	    disabledSkills,
    65	  }).filter((skill) => {
    66	    if (skill.mcpConfig) {
    67	      for (const mcpName of Object.keys(skill.mcpConfig)) {
    68	        if (systemMcpNames.has(mcpName)) return false
    69	      }
    70	    }
    71	    return true
    72	  })
    73	
    74	  const includeClaudeSkills = pluginConfig.claude_code?.skills !== false
    75	  const [configSourceSkills, userSkills, globalSkills, projectSkills, opencodeProjectSkills, agentsProjectSkills, agentsGlobalSkills] =
    76	    await Promise.all([
    77	      discoverConfigSourceSkills({
    78	        config: pluginConfig.skills,
    79	        configDir: directory,
    80	      }),
    81	      includeClaudeSkills ? discoverUserClaudeSkills() : Promise.resolve([]),
    82	      discoverOpencodeGlobalSkills(),
    83	      includeClaudeSkills ? discoverProjectClaudeSkills(directory) : Promise.resolve([]),
    84	      discoverOpencodeProjectSkills(directory),
    85	      discoverProjectAgentsSkills(directory),
    86	      discoverGlobalAgentsSkills(),
    87	    ])
    88	
    89	  const filteredConfigSourceSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
    90	    configSourceSkills,
    91	    browserProvider,
    92	  )
    93	  const filteredUserSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(userSkills, browserProvider)
    94	  const filteredGlobalSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(globalSkills, browserProvider)
    95	  const filteredProjectSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(projectSkills, browserProvider)
    96	  const filteredOpencodeProjectSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
    97	    opencodeProjectSkills,
    98	    browserProvider,
    99	  )
   100	  const filteredAgentsProjectSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
   101	    agentsProjectSkills,
   102	    browserProvider,
   103	  )
   104	  const filteredAgentsGlobalSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
   105	    agentsGlobalSkills,
   106	    browserProvider,
   107	  )
   108	
   109	  const mergedSkills = mergeSkills(
   110	    builtinSkills,
   111	    pluginConfig.skills,
   112	    filteredConfigSourceSkills,
   113	    [...filteredUserSkills, ...filteredAgentsGlobalSkills],
   114	    filteredGlobalSkills,
   115	    [...filteredProjectSkills, ...filteredAgentsProjectSkills],
   116	    filteredOpencodeProjectSkills,
   117	    { configDir: directory },
   118	  )
   119	
   120	  const availableSkills: AvailableSkill[] = mergedSkills.map((skill) => ({
   121	    name: skill.name,
   122	    description: skill.definition.description ?? "",
   123	    location: mapScopeToLocation(skill.scope),
   124	  }))
   125	
   126	  return {
   127	    mergedSkills,
   128	    availableSkills,
   129	    browserProvider,
   130	    disabledSkills,
   131	  }
   132	}

     1	import type { AvailableSkill } from "../dynamic-agent-prompt-builder"
     2	import type { BrowserAutomationProvider } from "../../config/schema"
     3	import type { LoadedSkill, SkillScope } from "../../features/opencode-skill-loader/types"
     4	import { createBuiltinSkills } from "../../features/builtin-skills"
     5	
     6	function mapScopeToLocation(scope: SkillScope): AvailableSkill["location"] {
     7	  if (scope === "user" || scope === "opencode") return "user"
     8	  if (scope === "project" || scope === "opencode-project") return "project"
     9	  return "plugin"
    10	}
    11	
    12	export function buildAvailableSkills(
    13	  discoveredSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    14	  browserProvider?: BrowserAutomationProvider,
    15	  disabledSkills?: Set<string>
    16	): AvailableSkill[] {
    17	  const builtinSkills = createBuiltinSkills({ browserProvider, disabledSkills })
    18	  const builtinSkillNames = new Set(builtinSkills.map(s => s.name))
    19	
    20	  const builtinAvailable: AvailableSkill[] = builtinSkills.map((skill) => ({
    21	    name: skill.name,
    22	    description: skill.description,
    23	    location: "plugin" as const,
    24	  }))
    25	
    26	  const discoveredAvailable: AvailableSkill[] = discoveredSkills
    27	    .filter(s => !builtinSkillNames.has(s.name) && !disabledSkills?.has(s.name))
    28	    .map((skill) => ({
    29	      name: skill.name,
    30	      description: skill.definition.description ?? "",
    31	      location: mapScopeToLocation(skill.scope),
    32	    }))
    33	
    34	  return [...builtinAvailable, ...discoveredAvailable]
    35	}
    36

     5	  description: string
     6	  metadata: AgentPromptMetadata
     7	}

    10	  name: string
    11	  category: "lsp" | "ast" | "search" | "session" | "command" | "other"
    12	}

    26	export function categorizeTools(toolNames: string[]): AvailableTool[] {
    27	  return toolNames.map((name) => {
    28	    let category: AvailableTool["category"] = "other"
    29	    if (name.startsWith("lsp_")) {
    30	      category = "lsp"
    31	    } else if (name.startsWith("ast_grep")) {
    32	      category = "ast"
    33	    } else if (name === "grep" || name === "glob") {
    34	      category = "search"
    35	    } else if (name.startsWith("session_")) {
    36	      category = "session"
    37	    } else if (name === "skill") {
    38	      category = "command"
    39	    }
    40	    return { name, category }
    41	  })
    42	}
    43	
    44	function formatToolsForPrompt(tools: AvailableTool[]): string {
    45	  const lspTools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === "lsp")
    46	  const astTools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === "ast")
    47	  const searchTools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === "search")
    48	
    49	  const parts: string[] = []
    50	
    51	  if (searchTools.length > 0) {
    52	    parts.push(...searchTools.map((t) => `\`${t.name}\``))
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  if (lspTools.length > 0) {
    56	    parts.push("`lsp_*`")
    57	  }
    58	
    59	  if (astTools.length > 0) {
    60	    parts.push("`ast_grep`")
    61	  }
    62	
    63	  return parts.join(", ")
    64	}
    65	
    66	export function buildKeyTriggersSection(agents: AvailableAgent[], _skills: AvailableSkill[] = []): string {
    67	  const keyTriggers = agents
    68	    .filter((a) => a.metadata.keyTrigger)
    69	    .map((a) => `- ${a.metadata.keyTrigger}`)
    70	
    71	  if (keyTriggers.length === 0) return ""
    72	
    73	  return `### Key Triggers (check BEFORE classification):
    74	
    75	${keyTriggers.join("\n")}
    76	- **"Look into" + "create PR"** → Not just research. Full implementation cycle expected.`
    77	}
    78	
    79	export function buildToolSelectionTable(
    80	  agents: AvailableAgent[],
    81	  tools: AvailableTool[] = [],
    82	  _skills: AvailableSkill[] = []
    83	): string {
    84	  const rows: string[] = [
    85	    "### Tool & Agent Selection:",
    86	    "",
    87	  ]
    88	
    89	  if (tools.length > 0) {
    90	    const toolsDisplay = formatToolsForPrompt(tools)
    91	    rows.push(`- ${toolsDisplay} — **FREE** — Not Complex, Scope Clear, No Implicit Assumptions`)
    92	  }
    93	
    94	  const costOrder = { FREE: 0, CHEAP: 1, EXPENSIVE: 2 }
    95	  const sortedAgents = [...agents]
    96	    .filter((a) => a.metadata.category !== "utility")
    97	    .sort((a, b) => costOrder[a.metadata.cost] - costOrder[b.metadata.cost])
    98	
    99	  for (const agent of sortedAgents) {
   100	    const shortDesc = agent.description.split(".")[0] || agent.description
   101	    rows.push(`- \`${agent.name}\` agent — **${agent.metadata.cost}** — ${shortDesc}`)
   102	  }
   103	
   104	  rows.push("")
   105	  rows.push("**Default flow**: explore/librarian (background) + tools → oracle (if required)")
   106	
   107	  return rows.join("\n")
   108	}
   109	
   110	export function buildExploreSection(agents: AvailableAgent[]): string {
   111	  const exploreAgent = agents.find((a) => a.name === "explore")
   112	  if (!exploreAgent) return ""
   113	
   114	  const useWhen = exploreAgent.metadata.useWhen || []
   115	  const avoidWhen = exploreAgent.metadata.avoidWhen || []
   116	
   117	  return `### Explore Agent = Contextual Grep
   118	
   119	Use it as a **peer tool**, not a fallback. Fire liberally for discovery, not for files you already know.
   120	
   121	**Delegation Trust Rule:** Once you fire an explore agent for a search, do **not** manually perform that same search yourself. Use direct tools only for non-overlapping work or when you intentionally skipped delegation.
   122	
   123	**Use Direct Tools when:**
   124	${avoidWhen.map((w) => `- ${w}`).join("\n")}
   125	
   126	**Use Explore Agent when:**
   127	${useWhen.map((w) => `- ${w}`).join("\n")}`
   128	}

   163	export function buildCategorySkillsDelegationGuide(categories: AvailableCategory[], skills: AvailableSkill[]): string {
   164	  if (categories.length === 0 && skills.length === 0) return ""
   165	
   166	  const categoryRows = categories.map((c) => {
   167	    const desc = c.description || c.name
   168	    return `- \`${c.name}\` — ${desc}`
   169	  })
   170	
   171	  const builtinSkills = skills.filter((s) => s.location === "plugin")
   172	  const customSkills = skills.filter((s) => s.location !== "plugin")
   173	
   174	  const builtinNames = builtinSkills.map((s) => s.name).join(", ")
   175	  const customNames = customSkills.map((s) => {
   176	    const source = s.location === "project" ? "project" : "user"
   177	    return `${s.name} (${source})`
   178	  }).join(", ")
   179	
   180	  let skillsSection: string
   181	
   182	  if (customSkills.length > 0 && builtinSkills.length > 0) {
   183	    skillsSection = `#### Available Skills (via \`skill\` tool)
   184	
   185	**Built-in**: ${builtinNames}
   186	**⚡ YOUR SKILLS (PRIORITY)**: ${customNames}
   187	
   188	> User-installed skills OVERRIDE built-in defaults. ALWAYS prefer YOUR SKILLS when domain matches.
   189	> Full skill descriptions → use the \`skill\` tool to check before EVERY delegation.`
   190	  } else if (customSkills.length > 0) {
   191	    skillsSection = `#### Available Skills (via \`skill\` tool)
   192	
   193	**⚡ YOUR SKILLS (PRIORITY)**: ${customNames}
   194	
   195	> User-installed skills OVERRIDE built-in defaults. ALWAYS prefer YOUR SKILLS when domain matches.

import type { BuiltinSkill } from "./types"
import type { BrowserAutomationProvider } from "../../config/schema"

import {
  playwrightSkill,
  agentBrowserSkill,
  playwrightCliSkill,
  frontendUiUxSkill,
  gitMasterSkill,
  devBrowserSkill,
  reviewWorkSkill,
  aiSlopRemoverSkill,
} from "./skills/index"

export interface CreateBuiltinSkillsOptions {
  browserProvider?: BrowserAutomationProvider
  disabledSkills?: Set<string>
}

export function createBuiltinSkills(options: CreateBuiltinSkillsOptions = {}): BuiltinSkill[] {
  const { browserProvider = "playwright", disabledSkills } = options

  let browserSkill: BuiltinSkill
  if (browserProvider === "agent-browser") {
    browserSkill = agentBrowserSkill
  } else if (browserProvider === "playwright-cli") {
    browserSkill = playwrightCliSkill
  } else {
    browserSkill = playwrightSkill
  }

  const skills = [browserSkill, frontendUiUxSkill, gitMasterSkill, devBrowserSkill, reviewWorkSkill, aiSlopRemoverSkill]

  if (!disabledSkills) {
    return skills
  }

  return skills.filter((skill) => !disabledSkills.has(skill.name))
}
import { createBuiltinSkills } from "../builtin-skills/skills"
import { discoverSkills } from "./loader"
import type { LoadedSkill } from "./types"
import type { SkillResolutionOptions } from "./skill-resolution-options"

const cachedSkillsByProvider = new Map<string, LoadedSkill[]>()

export function clearSkillCache(): void {
	cachedSkillsByProvider.clear()
}

export async function getAllSkills(options?: SkillResolutionOptions): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> {
	const cacheKey = options?.browserProvider ?? "playwright"
	const hasDisabledSkills = options?.disabledSkills && options.disabledSkills.size > 0

	// Skip cache if disabledSkills is provided (varies between calls)
	if (!hasDisabledSkills) {
		const cached = cachedSkillsByProvider.get(cacheKey)
		if (cached) return cached
	}

	const [discoveredSkills, builtinSkillDefinitions] = await Promise.all([
		discoverSkills({ includeClaudeCodePaths: true, directory: options?.directory }),
		Promise.resolve(
			createBuiltinSkills({
				browserProvider: options?.browserProvider,
				disabledSkills: options?.disabledSkills,
			})
		),
	])

	const builtinSkillsAsLoaded: LoadedSkill[] = builtinSkillDefinitions.map((skill) => ({
		name: skill.name,
		definition: {
			name: skill.name,
			description: skill.description,
			template: skill.template,
			model: skill.model,
			agent: skill.agent,
			subtask: skill.subtask,
		},
		scope: "builtin" as const,
		license: skill.license,
		compatibility: skill.compatibility,
		metadata: skill.metadata as Record<string, string> | undefined,
		allowedTools: skill.allowedTools,
		mcpConfig: skill.mcpConfig,
	}))

	// Provider-gated skill names that should be filtered based on browserProvider
	const providerGatedSkillNames = new Set(["agent-browser", "playwright"])
	const browserProvider = options?.browserProvider ?? "playwright"

	// Filter discovered skills to exclude provider-gated names that don't match the selected provider
	const filteredDiscoveredSkills = discoveredSkills.filter((skill) => {
		if (!providerGatedSkillNames.has(skill.name)) {
			return true
		}
		// For provider-gated skills, only include if it matches the selected provider
		return skill.name === browserProvider
	})

	const discoveredNames = new Set(filteredDiscoveredSkills.map((skill) => skill.name))
	const uniqueBuiltins = builtinSkillsAsLoaded.filter((skill) => !discoveredNames.has(skill.name))

	let allSkills = [...filteredDiscoveredSkills, ...uniqueBuiltins]

	// Filter discovered skills by disabledSkills (builtin skills are already filtered by createBuiltinSkills)
	if (hasDisabledSkills) {
		allSkills = allSkills.filter((skill) => !options!.disabledSkills!.has(skill.name))
	} else {
		cachedSkillsByProvider.set(cacheKey, allSkills)
	}

	return allSkills
}

     9	
    10	export interface MergeSkillsOptions {
    11	  configDir?: string
    12	}
    13	
    14	export function mergeSkills(
    15	  builtinSkills: BuiltinSkill[],
    16	  config: SkillsConfig | undefined,
    17	  configSourceSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    18	  userClaudeSkills: LoadedSkill[],

    21	  projectOpencodeSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    22	  options: MergeSkillsOptions = {}
    23	): LoadedSkill[] {
    24	  const skillMap = new Map<string, LoadedSkill>()
    25	
    26	  for (const builtin of builtinSkills) {
    27	    const loaded = builtinToLoadedSkill(builtin)
    28	    skillMap.set(loaded.name, loaded)
    29	  }
    30	
    31	  const normalizedConfig = normalizeSkillsConfig(config)
    32	
    33	  for (const [name, entry] of Object.entries(normalizedConfig.entries)) {
    34	    if (entry === false) continue
    35	    if (entry === true) continue
    36	
    37	    if (entry.disable) continue
    38	
    39	    const loaded = configEntryToLoadedSkill(name, entry, options.configDir)
    40	    if (loaded) {
    41	      const existing = skillMap.get(name)
    42	      if (existing && !entry.template && !entry.from) {
    43	        skillMap.set(name, mergeSkillDefinitions(existing, entry))
    44	      } else {
    45	        skillMap.set(name, loaded)
    46	      }
    47	    }
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  const fileSystemSkills = [
    51	    ...configSourceSkills,
    52	    ...userClaudeSkills,
    53	    ...userOpencodeSkills,
    54	    ...projectClaudeSkills,
    55	    ...projectOpencodeSkills,
    56	  ]
    57	
    58	  for (const skill of fileSystemSkills) {
    59	    const existing = skillMap.get(skill.name)
    60	    if (!existing || SCOPE_PRIORITY[skill.scope] > SCOPE_PRIORITY[existing.scope]) {
    61	      skillMap.set(skill.name, skill)
    62	    }
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  for (const [name, entry] of Object.entries(normalizedConfig.entries)) {
    66	    if (entry === true) continue
    67	    if (entry === false) {
    68	      skillMap.delete(name)
    69	      continue
    70	    }
    71	    if (entry.disable) {
    72	      skillMap.delete(name)
    73	      continue
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    const existing = skillMap.get(name)
    77	    if (existing && !entry.template && !entry.from) {
    78	      skillMap.set(name, mergeSkillDefinitions(existing, entry))
    79	    }
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  for (const name of normalizedConfig.disable) {
    83	    skillMap.delete(name)
    84	  }
    85	
    86	  if (normalizedConfig.enable.length > 0) {
    87	    const enableSet = new Set(normalizedConfig.enable)
    88	    for (const name of skillMap.keys()) {
    89	      if (!enableSet.has(name)) {
    90	        skillMap.delete(name)
    91	      }
    92	    }
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  return Array.from(skillMap.values())
    96	}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/src/features/opencode-skill-loader/skill-name-alias.ts --file_text 'import type { SkillScope } from "./types"

const scopePriority: Record<SkillScope, number> = {
  project: 4,
  user: 3,
  opencode: 2,
  "opencode-project": 2,
  plugin: 1,
  config: 1,
  builtin: 1,
}

type ResolvableSkill = {
  name: string
  scope?: SkillScope
}

export function getSkillShortName(skillName: string): string {
  const slashIndex = skillName.lastIndexOf("/")
  return slashIndex === -1 ? skillName : skillName.slice(slashIndex + 1)
}

function normalizeForCompare(name: string): string {
  return name.toLowerCase()
}

function skillInvocationCandidates(name: string): string[] {
  const withoutLeadingSlash = name.replace(/^\//, "")
  const candidates = [withoutLeadingSlash]

  if (withoutLeadingSlash.includes(":") && !withoutLeadingSlash.includes("/")) {
    candidates.push(withoutLeadingSlash.replace(":", "/"))
  }

  return candidates
}

function priorityOf(skill: ResolvableSkill): number {
  return skill.scope ? scopePriority[skill.scope] ?? 0 : 0
}

export function findSkillByResolvableName<T extends ResolvableSkill>(
  skills: T[],
  requestedName: string
): T | undefined {
  const candidates = skillInvocationCandidates(requestedName).map(normalizeForCompare)

  const exactMatch = skills.find((skill) =>
    candidates.includes(normalizeForCompare(skill.name))
  )
  if (exactMatch) return exactMatch

  const normalizedShortRequest = normalizeForCompare(requestedName.replace(/^\//, ""))
  if (normalizedShortRequest.includes("/") || normalizedShortRequest.includes(":")) {
    return undefined
  }

  return skills
    .filter((skill) => normalizeForCompare(getSkillShortName(skill.name)) === normalizedShortRequest)
    .sort((a, b) => priorityOf(b) - priorityOf(a))[0]
}
'

     1	import { readFileSync } from "node:fs"
     2	import { parseFrontmatter } from "../../shared/frontmatter"
     3	import type { LoadedSkill } from "./types"
     4	
     5	export function extractSkillTemplate(skill: LoadedSkill): string {
     6	  if (skill.scope === "config" && skill.definition.template) {
     7	    return skill.definition.template
     8	  }
     9	
    10	  if (skill.path) {
    11	    const content = readFileSync(skill.path, "utf-8")

    14	        }

    16	}

     1	import type { SkillScope } from "./types"
     2	
     3	const scopePriority: Record<SkillScope, number> = {
     4	  project: 4,
     5	  user: 3,
     6	  opencode: 2,
     7	  "opencode-project": 2,
     8	  config: 1,
     9	  builtin: 1,
    10	}
    11	
    12	type ResolvableSkill = {
    13	  name: string
    14	  scope?: SkillScope
    15	}
    16	
    17	export function getSkillShortName(skillName: string): string {
    18	  const slashIndex = skillName.lastIndexOf("/")
    19	  return slashIndex === -1 ? skillName : skillName.slice(slashIndex + 1)
    20	}
    21	
    22	function normalizeForCompare(name: string): string {
    23	  return name.toLowerCase()
    24	}
    25	
    26	function skillInvocationCandidates(name: string): string[] {
    27	  const withoutLeadingSlash = name.replace(/^\//, "")
    28	  const candidates = [withoutLeadingSlash]
    29	
    30	  if (withoutLeadingSlash.includes(":") && !withoutLeadingSlash.includes("/")) {
    31	    candidates.push(withoutLeadingSlash.replace(":", "/"))
    32	  }
    33	
    34	  return candidates
    35	}
    36	
    37	function priorityOf(skill: ResolvableSkill): number {
    38	  return skill.scope ? scopePriority[skill.scope] ?? 0 : 0
    39	}
    40	
    41	export function findSkillByResolvableName<T extends ResolvableSkill>(
    42	  skills: T[],
    43	  requestedName: string
    44	): T | undefined {
    45	  const candidates = skillInvocationCandidates(requestedName).map(normalizeForCompare)
    46	
    47	  const exactMatch = skills.find((skill) =>
    48	    candidates.includes(normalizeForCompare(skill.name))
    49	  )
    50	  if (exactMatch) return exactMatch
    51	
    52	  const normalizedShortRequest = normalizeForCompare(requestedName.replace(/^\//, ""))
    53	  if (normalizedShortRequest.includes("/") || normalizedShortRequest.includes(":")) {
    54	    return undefined
    55	  }
    56	
    57	  return skills
    58	    .filter((skill) => normalizeForCompare(getSkillShortName(skill.name)) === normalizedShortRequest)
    59	    .sort((a, b) => priorityOf(b) - priorityOf(a))[0]
    60	}

+import type { SkillScope } from "./types"
+
+const scopePriority: Record<SkillScope, number> = {
+  project: 4,
+  user: 3,
+  opencode: 2,
+  "opencode-project": 2,
+  config: 1,
+  builtin: 1,
+}
+
+type ResolvableSkill = {
+  name: string
+  scope?: SkillScope
+}
+
+export function getSkillShortName(skillName: string): string {
+  const slashIndex = skillName.lastIndexOf("/")
+  return slashIndex === -1 ? skillName : skillName.slice(slashIndex + 1)
+}
+
+function normalizeForCompare(name: string): string {
+  return name.toLowerCase()
+}
+
+function skillInvocationCandidates(name: string): string[] {
+  const withoutLeadingSlash = name.replace(/^\//, "")
+  const candidates = [withoutLeadingSlash]
+
+  if (withoutLeadingSlash.includes(":") && !withoutLeadingSlash.includes("/")) {
+    candidates.push(withoutLeadingSlash.replace(":", "/"))
+  }
+
+  return candidates
+}
+
+function priorityOf(skill: ResolvableSkill): number {
+  return skill.scope ? scopePriority[skill.scope] ?? 0 : 0
+}
+
+export function findSkillByResolvableName<T extends ResolvableSkill>(
+  skills: T[],
+  requestedName: string
+): T | undefined {
+  const candidates = skillInvocationCandidates(requestedName).map(normalizeForCompare)
+
+  const exactMatch = skills.find((skill) =>
+    candidates.includes(normalizeForCompare(skill.name))
+  )
+  if (exactMatch) return exactMatch
+
+  const normalizedShortRequest = normalizeForCompare(requestedName.replace(/^\//, ""))
+  if (normalizedShortRequest.includes("/") || normalizedShortRequest.includes(":")) {
+    return undefined
+  }
+
+  return skills
+    .filter((skill) => normalizeForCompare(getSkillShortName(skill.name)) === normalizedShortRequest)
+    .sort((a, b) => priorityOf(b) - priorityOf(a))[0]
+}
